9th-32nd Decklists
==================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on June 4, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to this event than just the [Top 8](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpams17/top-8-decklists-grand-prix-amsterdam-2017-06-04). Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9th through 32nd place. Almost all of them were at most one match win and/or a tiebreaker boost away from the Top 8.







#### Luis Gobern's Temur Aetherworks Marvel – 9th (12-2-1) at Grand Prix Amsterdam 2017


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
